This is very interesting. Let me trace through what happens:\n\n1. When `sendLocalReply` is called in the filter manager (lines 982-1050):\n   - It checks various conditions to decide how to send the reply\n   - If response hasn't started, it either calls `prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain` (line 1028) or `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain` (line 1031)\n\n2. In `prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain` (lines 1070-1094), the modify_headers function passed is:\n   ```cpp\n   [this, modify_headers](ResponseHeaderMap& headers) -> void {\n     if (streamInfo().route() && streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()) {\n       streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()->finalizeResponseHeaders(headers, streamInfo());\n     }\n     if (modify_headers) {\n       modify_headers(headers);\n     }\n   }\n   ```\n\n3. In `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain` (lines 1109-1130), the same pattern is used (lines 1123-1129)\n\nSo here's the issue! When the router filter calls `sendLocalReply`, it passes the `modify_headers_` lambda. But then in the filter manager's `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain`, it creates a NEW lambda that:\n1. Calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` from the route entry\n2. THEN calls the passed-in `modify_headers` function\n\nBut wait - the router's `modify_headers_` lambda doesn't call `finalizeResponseHeaders`. But when handling direct responses (lines 486-503), the router explicitly creates a lambda that calls `finalizeResponseHeaders` before passing it to `sendLocalReply`. This inconsistency suggests the cluster not found path might be missing the finalization step that direct responses get.\n\nHowever, there's another layer to consider: the filter manager's `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain` wraps any passed lambda in another lambda that also calls `finalizeResponseHeaders`. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01VHgVby1f3dsDQm8n5JfeN7","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_015mpsVoCtPjoY8diyYT2jTc","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/logs/agent/investigation.md","content":"# Investigation Report: Duplicate Response Headers in Envoy Filter Pipeline\n\n## Summary\n\nResponse headers configured via `response_headers_to_add` are being duplicated in certain local replies generated by the router filter. The root cause is a double invocation of `finalizeResponseHeaders()` — once by the filter manager's wrapping lambda (added in v1.35.0 to support response headers in local replies) and once by the router filter's own lambda for direct response entries.\n\n## Root Cause\n\n**Location**: Interaction between `source/common/router/router.cc` and `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`\n\n**Mechanism**:\n1. The router filter's direct response path (`router.cc:486-503`) passes a lambda to `sendLocalReply()` that explicitly calls `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (line 501)\n2. The filter manager's `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` method (`filter_manager.cc:1109-1130`) wraps this lambda in a new lambda that:\n   - First calls `streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (lines 1073-1074)\n   - Then calls the router's passed-in lambda (line 1077), which internally calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` again\n3. For certain routing configurations, both calls execute successfully, causing headers from `response_headers_to_add` to be added twice\n\n## Evidence\n\n### Router Filter - Direct Response Path\n**File**: `source/common/router/router.cc:486-503`\n```cpp\ncallbacks_->sendLocalReply(\n    direct_response->responseCode(), direct_response->responseBody(),\n    [this, direct_response, &request_headers = headers](Http::ResponseHeaderMap& response_headers) -> void {\n      // ...location header logic...\n      direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders(response_headers, callbacks_->streamInfo());  // FIRST CALL\n    },\n    absl::nullopt, StreamInfo::ResponseCodeDetails::get().DirectResponse);\n```\n\n### Filter Manager - sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain Wrapper\n**File**: `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc:1109-1130` and `1070-1094`\n```cpp\nUtility::sendLocalReply(\n    state_.destroyed_,\n    Utility::EncodeFunctions{\n        [this, modify_headers](ResponseHeaderMap& headers) -> void {\n          if (streamInfo().route() && streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()) {\n            streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()->finalizeResponseHeaders(headers, streamInfo());  // SECOND CALL\n          }\n          if (modify_headers) {\n            modify_headers(headers);  // This also calls finalizeResponseHeaders for direct response case\n          }\n        },\n        // ... other encode functions ...\n    },\n    Utility::LocalReplyData{...});\n```\n\n### Header Parser - How Headers Are Added\n**File**: `source/common/router/header_parser.cc:139-213`\n\nThe `evaluateHeaders()` method in `HeaderParser` processes each configured header based on its `append_action`:\n- `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`: Appends to existing header or adds if absent\n- `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`: Overwrites or adds if absent\n- `ADD_IF_ABSENT`: Only adds if header doesn't exist\n\nWhen `finalizeResponseHeaders()` calls `evaluateHeaders()`, it iterates through all configured headers and applies them. If called twice with the same headers map, headers with `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` will be appended twice.\n\n### Route Entry Implementation\n**File**: `source/common/router/config_impl.h:628-630`\n\n`RouteEntryImplBase` inherits from both `RouteEntryAndRoute` and `DirectResponseEntry`, making it simultaneously a route entry and direct response entry. This dual inheritance is central to the issue.\n\n## Affected Components\n\n1. **source/common/router/router.cc**\n   - `Filter::decodeHeaders()` — Initializes route and determines if direct response exists\n   - `Filter::onUpstreamAbort()` — Sends local replies for timeout/connection failures (line 1403)\n   - Direct response handling path (lines 486-503)\n\n2. **source/common/http/filter_manager.cc**\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::sendLocalReply()` — Entry point for local reply handling (line 982)\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` — Wraps modify_headers callback (line 1055)\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` — Wraps modify_headers callback (line 1109)\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::sendDirectLocalReply()` — Wraps modify_headers callback (line 1147)\n\n3. **source/common/router/config_impl.cc**\n   - `RouteEntryImplBase::finalizeResponseHeaders()` — Evaluates header parsers (line 942)\n   - `RouteEntryImplBase::directResponseEntry()` — Returns `this` for direct responses (line 1287)\n   - `RouteEntryImplBase::routeEntry()` — Returns `nullptr` for direct responses (line 1297)\n\n4. **source/common/router/header_parser.cc**\n   - `HeaderParser::evaluateHeaders()` — Applies headers based on append_action (line 139)\n   - `HeadersToAddEntry` — Parses deprecated `append` field vs new `append_action` enum (line 53)\n\n5. **api/envoy/config/core/v3/**\n   - `HeaderValueOption` proto — Contains both deprecated `append: BoolValue` and new `append_action: enum`\n   - Proto default for `append_action` is `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`\n\n## Causal Chain\n\n1. **Symptom**: Access logs show duplicate response headers in local replies\n   - Example: `x-custom-trace: abc123` appears twice despite `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` config\n\n2. **Path to Root Cause**:\n   - Local reply is generated by router (timeout/error condition)\n   - Router calls `callbacks_->sendLocalReply(code, body, modify_headers_lambda, ...)`\n   - For direct response paths, the lambda includes `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n   - `sendLocalReply()` delegates to filter manager's `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()`\n   - Filter manager creates a wrapping lambda that adds another `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call\n   - Both calls execute, evaluating header parsers twice\n   - Headers with `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` (default) get appended twice\n\n3. **Enabling Change**: v1.35.0 added response header support for local replies\n   - Added `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call to filter manager's wrapping lambda (line 1074, 1125, 1158)\n   - This was intended to apply `response_headers_to_add` from route config to local replies\n   - Did not account for cases where the route's lambda already calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n\n## Interaction Between Components\n\n1. **Router Filter's Role**:\n   - Determines if route has direct response entry\n   - If yes, passes lambda to `sendLocalReply()` that calls `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n   - If no (normal route), passes `modify_headers_` lambda that only adds attempt count header\n\n2. **Filter Manager's Wrapping**:\n   - Receives the router's lambda as `modify_headers` parameter\n   - Creates a NEW lambda that calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` first (if route entry exists)\n   - Then calls the passed-in lambda\n   - This wrapping happens for both `prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` and `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()`\n\n3. **Header Parser Behavior**:\n   - Each call to `evaluateHeaders()` iterates through all configured headers\n   - Headers with `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` are appended via `headers.addReferenceKey()`\n   - When called twice on same headers map, appends happen twice\n   - Result: duplicated headers in the final response\n\n## Recommendation\n\n**Fix Strategy**: Prevent double invocation of `finalizeResponseHeaders()` by ensuring it's called exactly once per local reply response, regardless of whether the route is a direct response or regular route entry.\n\n**Options**:\n1. **Move responsibility to filter manager**: Remove `finalizeResponseHeaders()` calls from route lambdas and let filter manager handle all cases (safest approach)\n2. **Route-specific handling**: Check route type in filter manager before calling `finalizeResponseHeaders()` to avoid duplication\n3. **Callback deduplication**: Mark when `finalizeResponseHeaders()` has been called and skip second invocation\n4. **Validate append_action semantics**: Ensure `append_action` correctly enforces `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` behavior even on second call\n\n**Diagnostic Steps**:\n1. Enable debug logging in `HeaderParser::evaluateHeaders()` to track each invocation\n2. Add counters for `finalizeResponseHeaders()` calls per request in `StreamInfo`\n3. Monitor response header counts for local replies vs upstream responses\n4. Audit all code paths that call `sendLocalReply()` to identify which pass lambdas with embedded `finalizeResponseHeaders()` calls\n\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":6,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1192,"cache_read_input_tokens":104276,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1192},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"825b08ec-f84b-4d1f-b037-c1c026ba5d28","uuid":"e8350f3c-2247-46d6-b354-8766d8d327d1"}
